-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 214:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SedanLarge02_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SedanLarge02_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]
Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 215: Identify: the next "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonCity > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 216: Add: the "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_01 => "SedanLarge02"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: -15 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonCity_Mat_02_A

Then move "SedanLarge02" into the empty: "Vehicles" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 217: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge02" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 218: Add: "Camera" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "SedanLarge02Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "SedanLarge02Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 1.4 Z: -6.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 219: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge02" add empty as child named "WheelMeshes"

Set the Transform of "WheelMeshes":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Copy & paste the following meshes into "WheelMeshes" as children
(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr

Transforms should be fine and unaffected but, let us just mention them for
good measure.

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7449768 Y: 0.361439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7449768 Y: 0.361439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7449768 Y: 0.361439 Z: -1.24979 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7449768 Y: 0.361439 Z: -1.24979
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 220: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge02" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Wheels:
-------------

Front Wheels Collider Radius: 0.361439
Front Wheels Collider Position Y: 0.511439 (0.361439+0.15)  *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

Rear Wheels:
------------

Rear Wheels Collider Radius: 0.361439
Rear Wheels Collider Position Y: 0.511439 (0.361439+0.15)  *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.361439
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.361439

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7449768 Y: 0.511439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7449768 Y: 0.511439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Step 221: Add to: SedanLarge02 (SedanLarge02Controller.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SedanLarge02Controller.cs) to "SedanLarge02"

Adjust the following settings:

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: SedanLarge02 (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl (Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

In Rigidbody:
-------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 2000

Step 223: Add to: SedanLarge02 (SedanLarge02Entry.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SedanLarge02Entry.cs) to "SedanLarge02"

Adjust the following settings:


Game Objects:
-------------

SedanLarge02: SedanLarge02
Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: SedanLarge02_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to you
  likings and needs:

Center: X: -0.001805723 Y: 0.8131697 Z: 0.1403447
Size: X: 4.003421 Y: 1.174145 Z: 1.925263


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 224: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SedanLarge02Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge02Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text outputdisplay thus such would make sence to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

Step 226: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add IMG: "SedanLarge02_SpeedoNeedle"

Middle Center

Pos Y: -24

Width: 260
Height: 260


In: "Image"


Source Image: Speedometer-Needle

Color: (Suggested Hex) 6B3232

Step 227: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add TMP TEXT: "SedanLarge02_SpeedText"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SedanLarge02_SpeedText"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Pos Y: -120.4

Width: 200
Height: 50

Text Input:
-----------

0 mph


Font Size: 36 *

Vertex Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF

Alignment: Center Middle

Face:
Dilate: 0.21 *

Outline: YES
Thickness: 0.121 *

Underlay: YES
Dilate: 0.02 *
Softness: 0.522 *

* Note these are just suggestions for you then to tweak and adjust further to
  your likings.

Step 228: In Vehicles > SedanLarge02 attach script: (SedanLarge02Speedometer.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach SedanLarge02Speedometer script: (SedanLarge02Speedometer.cs) to
Vehicle: "SedanLarge02"

In: "SedanLarge02" > SedanLarge02 Speedometer (Script)

Adjust the minimal settings as far as what is min needed: (Needle IMG and
Speed Text)

Needle: SedanLarge02_Needle

Speed Text: SedanLarge02_SpeedText (Text Mesh Pro UGUI)

GameObjects:

Interface Parent Object: SedanLarge02_Speedometer
Interface IMG01 Object: SedanLarge02_SpeedoGuage
Interface IMG02 Object: SedanLarge02_SpeedoNeedle
Interface Text Object: SedanLarge02_SpeedText



Note: Lastly,  we need to disable
the listed objects found below as we do not want these objects to display
prior to awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by
default and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive
item in start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable
these objects in the editor.

Game Objects:

SedanLarge02Speedometer
SedanLarge02_SpeedoGuage
SedanLarge02_SpeedoNeedle
SedanLarge02_SpeedText

Step 229:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SedanLarge03_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SedanLarge03_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]
Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 230: Identify: the next "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonCity > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 231: Add: the "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_01 => "SedanLarge03"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: -9 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonCity_Mat_03_A

Then move "SedanLarge03" into the empty: "Vehicles" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 232: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge03" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Step 233: Add: "Camera" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "SedanLarge03Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "SedanLarge03Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 1.4 Z: -6.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Step 234: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set the Transform of "WheelMeshes":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr

Step 235: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge03" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Wheels:
-------------

Front Wheels Collider Radius: 0.361439
Front Wheels Collider Position Y: 0.511439 (0.361439+0.15)  *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

Rear Wheels:
------------

Rear Wheels Collider Radius: 0.361439
Rear Wheels Collider Position Y: 0.511439 (0.361439+0.15)  *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.361439
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.361439

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7449768 Y: 0.511439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Step 239: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SedanLarge03Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge03Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text outputdisplay thus such would make sence to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonCity > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 246: Add: the "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_01 => "SedanLarge04"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: -3 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonCity_Mat_04_A

Then move "SedanLarge04" into the empty: "Vehicles" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 247: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge04" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 248: Add: "Camera" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "SedanLarge04Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "SedanLarge04Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 1.4 Z: -6.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 249: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge04" add empty as child named "WheelMeshes"

Set the Transform of "WheelMeshes":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Copy & paste the following meshes into "WheelMeshes" as children
(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr

Transforms should be fine and unaffected but, let us just mention them for
good measure.

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7449768 Y: 0.361439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7449768 Y: 0.361439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7449768 Y: 0.361439 Z: -1.24979 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7449768 Y: 0.361439 Z: -1.24979
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 250: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge04" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Wheels:
-------------

Front Wheels Collider Radius: 0.361439
Front Wheels Collider Position Y: 0.511439 (0.361439+0.15)  *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

Rear Wheels:
------------

Rear Wheels Collider Radius: 0.361439
Rear Wheels Collider Position Y: 0.511439 (0.361439+0.15)  *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.361439
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.361439

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7449768 Y: 0.511439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7449768 Y: 0.511439 Z: 1.632266
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7449768 Y: 0.511439 Z: -1.24979
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7449768 Y: 0.511439 Z: -1.24979

Step 251: Add to: SedanLarge04 (SedanLarge04Controller.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SedanLarge04Controller.cs) to "SedanLarge04"

Adjust the following settings:

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: SedanLarge04 (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl (Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Sedan_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

In Rigidbody:
-------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 2000

Step 253: Add to: SedanLarge04 (SedanLarge04Entry.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SedanLarge04Entry.cs) to "SedanLarge04"

Adjust the following settings:


Game Objects:
-------------

SedanLarge04: SedanLarge04
Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: SedanLarge04_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to you
  likings and needs:

Center: X: -0.001805723 Y: 0.8131697 Z: 0.1403447
Size: X: 4.003421 Y: 1.174145 Z: 1.925263


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 254: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SedanLarge04Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanLarge04Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text outputdisplay thus such would make sence to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 257: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add TMP TEXT: "SedanLarge04_SpeedText"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SedanLarge04_SpeedText"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Pos Y: -120.4

Width: 200
Height: 50

Text Input:
-----------

0 mph


Font Size: 36 *

Vertex Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF

Alignment: Center Middle

Face:
Dilate: 0.21 *

Outline: YES
Thickness: 0.121 *

Underlay: YES
Dilate: 0.02 *
Softness: 0.522 *

* Note these are just suggestions for you then to tweak and adjust further to
  your likings.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 258: In Vehicles > SedanLarge04 attach script: (SedanLarge04Speedometer.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach SedanLarge04Speedometer script: (SedanLarge04Speedometer.cs) to
Vehicle: "SedanLarge04"

In: "SedanLarge04" > SedanLarge04 Speedometer (Script)

Adjust the minimal settings as far as what is min needed: (Needle IMG and
Speed Text)

Needle: SedanLarge04_Needle

Speed Text: SedanLarge04_SpeedText (Text Mesh Pro UGUI)

GameObjects:

Interface Parent Object: SedanLarge04_Speedometer
Interface IMG01 Object: SedanLarge04_SpeedoGuage
Interface IMG02 Object: SedanLarge04_SpeedoNeedle
Interface Text Object: SedanLarge04_SpeedText



Note: Lastly,  we need to disable
the listed objects found below as we do not want these objects to display
prior to awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by
default and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive
item in start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable
these objects in the editor.

Game Objects:

SedanLarge04Speedometer
SedanLarge04_SpeedoGuage
SedanLarge04_SpeedoNeedle
SedanLarge04_SpeedText

Step 259:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SedanMedium01_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SedanMedium01_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]
Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 260: Identify: the next "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonCity > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 261: Add: the "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_01 => "SedanMedium01"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: 3 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonCity_Mat_01_A

Then move "SedanMedium01" into the empty: "Vehicles" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 262: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium01" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 263: Add: "Camera" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "SedanMedium01Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "SedanMedium01Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 1.4 Z: -6.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 264: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium01" add empty as child named "WheelMeshes"

Set the Transform of "WheelMeshes":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Copy & paste the following meshes into "WheelMeshes" as children
(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_rr

Transforms should be fine and unaffected but, let us just mention them for
good measure.


SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 265: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium01" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Wheels:
-------------

Front Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4186304
Front Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5686304 (0.4186304+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

Rear Wheels:
------------

Rear Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4186304
Rear Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5686304 (0.4186304+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4186304
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4186304

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.5686304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.5686304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.5686304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.5686304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: SedanMedium01 (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl (Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

In Rigidbody:
-------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 1500

Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: SedanMedium01_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to you
  likings and needs:

Center: X: -0.02273822 Y: 1.064519 Z: 0.03516877
Size: X: 4.073957 Y: 1.639387 Z: 1.641719

Step 270: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SedanMedium01Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium01Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text outputdisplay thus such would make sence to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  your likings.

Step 274: In Vehicles > SedanMedium01 attach script: (SedanMedium01Speedometer.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach SedanMedium01Speedometer script: (SedanMedium01Speedometer.cs) to
Vehicle: "SedanMedium01"

In: "SedanMedium01" > SedanMedium01 Speedometer (Script)

Adjust the minimal settings as far as what is min needed: (Needle IMG and
Speed Text)

Needle: SedanMedium01_Needle

Speed Text: SedanMedium01_SpeedText (Text Mesh Pro UGUI)

GameObjects:

Interface Parent Object: SedanMedium01_Speedometer
Interface IMG01 Object: SedanMedium01_SpeedoGuage
Interface IMG02 Object: SedanMedium01_SpeedoNeedle
Interface Text Object: SedanMedium01_SpeedText



Note: Lastly,  we need to disable
the listed objects found below as we do not want these objects to display
prior to awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by
default and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive
item in start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable
these objects in the editor.

Game Objects:

SedanMedium01Speedometer
SedanMedium01_SpeedoGuage
SedanMedium01_SpeedoNeedle
SedanMedium01_SpeedText

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 275:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SedanMedium02_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SedanMedium02_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]
Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 276: Identify: the next "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonCity > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 277: Add: the "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_01 => "SedanMedium02"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: 9 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonCity_Mat_02_A

Then move "SedanMedium02" into the empty: "Vehicles" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 278: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium02" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 279: Add: "Camera" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "SedanMedium02Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "SedanMedium02Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 1.4 Z: -6.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 280: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium02" add empty as child named "WheelMeshes"

Set the Transform of "WheelMeshes":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Copy & paste the following meshes into "WheelMeshes" as children
(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_rr

Transforms should be fine and unaffected but, let us just mention them for
good measure.


SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 281: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium02" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Wheels:
-------------

Front Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4186304
Front Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5686304 (0.4186304+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

Rear Wheels:
------------

Rear Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4186304
Rear Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5686304 (0.4186304+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4186304
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4186304

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.5686304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Adjust the following settings:

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: SedanMedium02 (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl (Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

In Rigidbody:
-------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 1500

Step 284: Add to: SedanMedium02 (SedanMedium02Entry.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SedanMedium02Entry.cs) to "SedanMedium02"

Adjust the following settings:


Game Objects:
-------------

SedanMedium02: SedanMedium02
Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: SedanMedium02_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to you
  likings and needs:

Center: X: -0.02273822 Y: 1.064519 Z: 0.03516877
Size: X: 4.073957 Y: 1.639387 Z: 1.641719


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 285: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SedanMedium02Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium02Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text outputdisplay thus such would make sence to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 288: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add TMP TEXT: "SedanMedium02_SpeedText"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SedanMedium02_SpeedText"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Pos Y: -120.4

Width: 200
Height: 50

Text Input:
-----------

0 mph


Font Size: 36 *

Vertex Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF

Alignment: Center Middle

Face:
Dilate: 0.21 *

Outline: YES
Thickness: 0.121 *

Underlay: YES
Dilate: 0.02 *
Softness: 0.522 *

* Note these are just suggestions for you then to tweak and adjust further to
  your likings.

Step 289: In Vehicles > SedanMedium02 attach script: (SedanMedium02Speedometer.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach SedanMedium02Speedometer script: (SedanMedium02Speedometer.cs) to
Vehicle: "SedanMedium02"

In: "SedanMedium02" > SedanMedium02 Speedometer (Script)

Adjust the minimal settings as far as what is min needed: (Needle IMG and
Speed Text)

Needle: SedanMedium02_Needle

Speed Text: SedanMedium02_SpeedText (Text Mesh Pro UGUI)

GameObjects:

Interface Parent Object: SedanMedium02_Speedometer
Interface IMG01 Object: SedanMedium02_SpeedoGuage
Interface IMG02 Object: SedanMedium02_SpeedoNeedle
Interface Text Object: SedanMedium02_SpeedText



Note: Lastly,  we need to disable
the listed objects found below as we do not want these objects to display
prior to awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by
default and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive
item in start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable
these objects in the editor.

Game Objects:

SedanMedium02Speedometer
SedanMedium02_SpeedoGuage
SedanMedium02_SpeedoNeedle
SedanMedium02_SpeedText

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 290:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SedanMedium03_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SedanMedium03_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]
Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 291: Identify: the next "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonCity > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 292: Add: the "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_01 => "SedanMedium03"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: 15 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonCity_Mat_03_A

Then move "SedanMedium03" into the empty: "Vehicles" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 293: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium03" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 294: Add: "Camera" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "SedanMedium03Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "SedanMedium03Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 1.4 Z: -6.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 295: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium03" add empty as child named "WheelMeshes"

Set the Transform of "WheelMeshes":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Copy & paste the following meshes into "WheelMeshes" as children
(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_rr

Transforms should be fine and unaffected but, let us just mention them for
good measure.


SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 296: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium03" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Wheels:
-------------

Front Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4186304
Front Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5686304 (0.4186304+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

Rear Wheels:
------------

Rear Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4186304
Rear Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5686304 (0.4186304+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4186304
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4186304

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.5686304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr

Step 299: Add to: SedanMedium03 (SedanMedium03Entry.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SedanMedium03Entry.cs) to "SedanMedium03"

Adjust the following settings:


Game Objects:
-------------

SedanMedium03: SedanMedium03
Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: SedanMedium03_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to you
  likings and needs:

Center: X: -0.02273822 Y: 1.064519 Z: 0.03516877
Size: X: 4.073957 Y: 1.639387 Z: 1.641719


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 300: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SedanMedium03Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium03Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text outputdisplay thus such would make sence to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 303: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add TMP TEXT: "SedanMedium03_SpeedText"

---------------

Height: 50

-----------

0 mph

Face:
Dilate: 0.21 *

Outline: YES
Thickness: 0.121 *

Underlay: YES
Dilate: 0.02 *
Softness: 0.522 *

* Note these are just suggestions for you then to tweak and adjust further to
  your likings.

Step 304: In Vehicles > SedanMedium03 attach script: (SedanMedium03Speedometer.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach SedanMedium03Speedometer script: (SedanMedium03Speedometer.cs) to
Vehicle: "SedanMedium03"

In: "SedanMedium03" > SedanMedium03 Speedometer (Script)

Adjust the minimal settings as far as what is min needed: (Needle IMG and
Speed Text)

Needle: SedanMedium03_Needle

Speed Text: SedanMedium03_SpeedText (Text Mesh Pro UGUI)

GameObjects:

Interface Parent Object: SedanMedium03_Speedometer
Interface IMG01 Object: SedanMedium03_SpeedoGuage
Interface IMG02 Object: SedanMedium03_SpeedoNeedle
Interface Text Object: SedanMedium03_SpeedText



Note: Lastly,  we need to disable
the listed objects found below as we do not want these objects to display
prior to awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by
default and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive
item in start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable
these objects in the editor.

Game Objects:

SedanMedium03Speedometer
SedanMedium03_SpeedoGuage
SedanMedium03_SpeedoNeedle
SedanMedium03_SpeedText

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 305:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SedanMedium04_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SedanMedium04_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]
Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 306: Identify: the next "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonCity > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 307: Add: the "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_01 => "SedanMedium04"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: 21 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonCity_Mat_04_A

Then move "SedanMedium04" into the empty: "Vehicles" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 308: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium04" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 309: Add: "Camera" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "SedanMedium04Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "SedanMedium04Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 1.4 Z: -6.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 310: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium04" add empty as child named "WheelMeshes"

Set the Transform of "WheelMeshes":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Copy & paste the following meshes into "WheelMeshes" as children
(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Armored_Car_Wheel_rr

Transforms should be fine and unaffected but, let us just mention them for
good measure.


SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7690811 Y: 0.4186304 Z: -1.442807
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 311: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium04" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Wheels:
-------------

Front Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4186304
Front Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5686304 (0.4186304+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

Rear Wheels:
------------

Rear Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4186304
Rear Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5686304 (0.4186304+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4186304
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4186304

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7690811 Y: 0.5686304 Z: 1.500103
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Step 312: Add to: SedanMedium04 (SedanMedium04Controller.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SedanMedium04Controller.cs) to "SedanMedium04"

Adjust the following settings:

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: SedanMedium04 (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl (Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Medium_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

In Rigidbody:
-------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 1500

Step 314: Add to: SedanMedium04 (SedanMedium04Entry.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SedanMedium04Entry.cs) to "SedanMedium04"

Adjust the following settings:


Game Objects:
-------------

SedanMedium04: SedanMedium04
Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: SedanMedium04_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to you
  likings and needs:

Center: X: -0.02273822 Y: 1.064519 Z: 0.03516877
Size: X: 4.073957 Y: 1.639387 Z: 1.641719


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 315: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SedanMedium04Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SedanMedium04Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text outputdisplay thus such would make sence to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Height: 260


In: "Image"


Source Image: Speedometer-Needle

Color: (Suggested Hex) 6B3232


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 318: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add TMP TEXT: "SedanMedium04_SpeedText"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SedanMedium04_SpeedText"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Pos Y: -120.4

Width: 200
Height: 50

Text Input:
-----------

0 mph


Font Size: 36 *

Vertex Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF

Alignment: Center Middle

Face:
Dilate: 0.21 *

Outline: YES
Thickness: 0.121 *

Underlay: YES
Dilate: 0.02 *
Softness: 0.522 *

* Note these are just suggestions for you then to tweak and adjust further to
  your likings.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 319: In Vehicles > SedanMedium04 attach script: (SedanMedium04Speedometer.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach SedanMedium04Speedometer script: (SedanMedium04Speedometer.cs) to
Vehicle: "SedanMedium04"

In: "SedanMedium04" > SedanMedium04 Speedometer (Script)

Adjust the minimal settings as far as what is min needed: (Needle IMG and
Speed Text)

Needle: SedanMedium04_Needle

Speed Text: SedanMedium04_SpeedText (Text Mesh Pro UGUI)

GameObjects:

Interface Parent Object: SedanMedium04_Speedometer
Interface IMG01 Object: SedanMedium04_SpeedoGuage
Interface IMG02 Object: SedanMedium04_SpeedoNeedle
Interface Text Object: SedanMedium04_SpeedText



Note: Lastly,  we need to disable
the listed objects found below as we do not want these objects to display
prior to awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by
default and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive
item in start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable
these objects in the editor.

Game Objects:

SedanMedium04Speedometer
SedanMedium04_SpeedoGuage
SedanMedium04_SpeedoNeedle
SedanMedium04_SpeedText
